  205. newh =  (e.gh[ix] * m) + (e.tabh + e.thumbh);↩
  206. } ↩
  207. if(window.rs_init_css===undefined) window.rs_init_css = document.head.appendChild(document.createElement("style")); ↩
  208. document.getElementById(e.c).height = newh+"px";↩
  209. window.rs_init_css.innerHTML += "#"+e.c+"_wrapper { height: "+newh+"px }"; ↩
  210. } catch(e){↩
  211. console.log("Failure at Presize of Slider:" + e)↩
  212. }   ↩
  213. //});↩
  214.   };</script>↩
  215. <link rel="stylesheet" id="et-divi-customizer-global-cached-inline-styles" href="https://www.bawitex-wil.ch/wp-content/et-cache/global/et-divi-customizer-global.min.css?ver=1649003604" /></head>↩
